<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/createcollection \{#operation-createcollection\}

</OperationTitleSection>

_Create Collection_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### audienceFilters \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

A list of filters for the query. An AND is assumed between different facetFilters. For example, owner Sumeet and type Spreadsheet shows documents that are by Sumeet AND are Spreadsheets.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  parentId="audienceFilters_FacetFilter"

  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-createcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

##### groupName \{#operation-editcollection+request+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### groupName \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+groupname\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Indicates the value of a facet, if any, that the given facet is grouped under. This is only used for nested facets, for example, fieldName could be owner and groupName would be Spreadsheet if showing all owners for spreadsheets as a nested facet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<ExpandablePropertyExamples slot="examples">

_Example:_

```
Spreadsheet
```

</ExpandablePropertyExamples>

</ExpandableProperty>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### values \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+audiencefilters+facetfilter+values\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Within a single FacetFilter, the values are to be treated like an OR. For example, fieldName type with values [EQUALS Presentation, EQUALS Spreadsheet] means we want to show a document if it's a Presentation OR a Spreadsheet.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+creator+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

  typeAnnotations={[]}
  hasFrontMatter={true}
  expandByDefault={false}
>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### permissions \{#operation-editcollection+responses+200+application-json+updatedby+metadata+permissions\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Describes the permissions levels that a user has for permissioned features. When the client sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the additional permissions granted to a user on top of what they have via their roles.
When the server sends this, Permissions.read and Permissions.write are the complete (merged) set of permissions the user has, and Permissions.roles is just for display purposes.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/editcollectionitem \{#operation-editcollectionitem\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Update Collection item_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Update the URL, Glean Document ID, description of an item within a Collection given its ID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /rest/api/v1/getcollection \{#operation-getcollection\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Read Collection_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Read the details of a Collection given its ID. Does not fetch items in this Collection.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

##### trackingToken \{#operation-getcollection+responses+200+application-json+trackingtoken\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>
